! ============ !
! Proper nouns !
! ============ !

! Note: the final non-sámi consonants: 
!          b  d  g  h  m  n  p  z
! write as b3 d3 g3 h3 m3 n3 p3 z3

! Table of content
! ----------------
! Continuation lexica
! Personal names
!  First names
!  Surnames
! Place names
! ----------------

! Continuation lexica
! ===================

! Some of the entries point to continuation lexica in the sme-lex.txt
! file, such as GOAHTI. This implies that names have the same inflection as
! ordinary nouns, which is probably not true. These lexica must thus be re-
! vised as soon as the lexica for names become more accurate.

! Continuation lexica for personal names
! --------------------------------------

! Vowel final names
! - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON ACCRA ! Vowel-final names without Gradation and Ill change
! These sublexica are irrelevant for ACCRA, but added
! for the sake of the lexicon MARJA
 ACCRA-NE ;
 ACCRA-I ;
 ACCRA-OBL ;
 ACCRA-IICASE ;
 DenominalAdjsC ;

LEXICON DEATNU ! Vowel final names with Gradation and Ill change (place names)
MARJA ;
! The separate lexicon was kept in case we need separate treatment
! of place and person in the future. Most MARJA entries are personal names, 
! and all DEATNU entries are placenames.

LEXICON MARJA ! Vowel-final names with Gradation and Ill change (person names)
 ACCRA-NE ;
 :X3 ACCRA-I ;
 :X4 ACCRA-OBL ;
 :X5 ACCRA-IICASE ;
 DenominalAdjsC ;

LEXICON GUOLBBA ! Trisyll. Inanim. Gradating 0-Nouns
 +N+Prop:X4 BOAZU- ;
 +N+Prop:X8 MALES ;		!^C^
 +N+Prop:X2 MALLAS- ;
! As SEAMU, but without derivation
 DenominalAdjsC ;

LEXICON ACCRA-NE
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;  ! To each Nom sg entry there is added an Attr tag
 +N+Prop+Sg+Attr: K ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: R ;  !^C^
 +N+Prop+Ess:n K ;
 +N+Prop+las1:laz1z1 DEARVVASLAS ;		!^C^

LEXICON ACCRA-I
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:j K ;

LEXICON ACCRA-OBL
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:# R ; ! for placenames  !^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:s K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:jn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:t K ;

LEXICON ACCRA-IICASE
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:jdda K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:jn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:jgujn K ;

! Vowel-final names where the final vowel carries
! primary or secondary stress. Monosyllables and
! Scandinavian stressed compounds in -V belong here.
LEXICON NYSTØ
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Attr: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: R ;			!^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:%:s K ; ! Nystø:s
     NYSTØ-OBL ;
 :%: NYSTØ-OBL ;
 :%- NYSTØ-OBL ;

LEXICON NYSTØ-OBL
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a# R ; ! for placenames !^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:aj K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:as K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:an K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:ajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:ajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:ajde K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:ajgujn K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:'1a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:'1a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:'1aj K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:'1as K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:'1ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:'an K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:'1at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:'1ajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:'1ajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:'1ajde K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:'1ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:'1ajgujn K ;
 +N+Prop+las1:laz1z1 DEARVVASLAS ;		!^C^

! Consonant-filal names
! - - - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON CNAME
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Attr: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom:# R ; ! for place names  !^C^
 +N+Prop+las1:alaz1z1 DEARVVASLAS ;		!^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:%:s K ; ! Tydal:s
     CNAME-OBL ;
 :%: CNAME-OBL ;
 :%- CNAME-OBL ;
 :%: CNAME-SUBSTANDARD ; ! XXX substandard
 :%- CNAME-SUBSTANDARD ; ! XXX substandard

LEXICON CNAME-OBL
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a R ; ! for place names !^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:ij K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc+isuf:is K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com+isuf:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess+isuf:in K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc+asuf:as K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com+asuf:ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess+asuf:an K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:ijdda K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:ijgujn K ;

LEXICON CNAME-SUBSTANDARD ! XXX substandard
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:i K ;! XXX substandard
 ! This is for "Statskog:i"


!checking for i- and a-base suffixes.

LEXICON PLACE-DIM
 +N+Prop: DIMINC ;


! Finnish Itkonen, lexicon for Finnish nen-names
LEXICON C-FI-NEN
 :nen3 CNAME ; ! In Norway, they are declined as CNAME
               ! with ordinary genitive Itkonena
 :s FI-S ;     ! In Finland, they are declined with
               ! Itkosa as the oblique stem.

! Finnish Itkosa
LEXICON FI-S
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:# R ; ! For names !^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:ij K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:is K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:in K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:ijdda K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:ijgujn K ;
 +N+Prop+las1:laz1z1 DEARVVASLAS ;		!^C^

LEXICON OLSEN ! Final foot structure (X.) and (X..) => Loc:is
! Different lexicon for personal surnames. 
LONDON ;

LEXICON LONDON ! Final foot structure (X.) and (X..) => Loc:is

 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Attr: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: R ;	!^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:ij K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:is K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:in K ;
 +N+Prop+las1:laz1z1 DEARVVASLAS ;		!^C^

LEXICON BERN ! Final foot structure (X) => Loc:as

 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Attr: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: R ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a R ;	!^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:ij K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:as K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:ain K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:an K ;
 +N+Prop+las1:alaz1z1 DEARVVASLAS ;		!^C^

LEXICON DUORTNUS ! Cns-final, cons.grad.
 +N+Prop:X4 MALIS0 ;
 +N+Prop:X8 MALES ;
 +N+Prop:X2 MALLAS- ;
 DenominalAdjsC ; 

LEXICON ANAR ! Cns-fin, no cons.grad.
 +N+Prop: MALIS0 ;
 +N+Prop:X7 MALES ;
 +N+Prop: MALLAS- ;
 DenominalAdjsC ; 

LEXICON HEANDARAT ! Bisyll. Non-Gradating C-Proper Names
 +N+Prop+Attr K ;
 +N+Prop:00 JOHTOLAT0 ;
 +N+Prop:a JOHTOLAHKA- ;
 +N+Prop+Dimin:aX6z1 DIMINC ;
 DenominalAdjsC ; 
 


LEXICON NIILLAS ! Trisyll. Non-Gradating C-Proper Names
 +N+Prop+Attr K ;
 +N+Prop: MALIS0 ;	! NE
 +N+Prop: MALLAS- ;	! Obl
 +N+Prop+s1+Dimin:az1z1 DIMINV ;


LEXICON GEAVNNIS
 +N+Prop:X4 MALIS0 ;
 +N+Prop:X8 MALES ;
 +N+Prop:Y5 FALLA- ;
 DenominalAdjsC ; 

! Plural lexica
! -------------

LEXICON ALEUHTAT
 +N+Prop+Ess:n K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:X4t K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:jde K ; ! 2-syll stem
 +N+Prop+Pl:X5 ALEUHTAT-OBL ;
 DenominalAdjsC ; 

LEXICON ALEUHTAT-OBL ! 2-syll stem
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:jn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:jgujn K ;

LEXICON SULLOT
 +N+Prop+Ess:X4n K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:Y5t K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:jde K ; ! 2-syll stem
 +N+Prop+Pl:Y6 ALEUHTAT-OBL ;
 DenominalAdjsC ; 

LEXICON EATNAMAT
 +N+Prop+Ess:X4n K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:X2at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:jdda K ; ! 3-syll stem
 +N+Prop+Pl:X2i ALEUHTAT-OBL ;
 DenominalAdjsC ;
